    def getOrder(self, order="inOrder"):
        def inOrder(root):
            if root:
                inOrder(root.left)
                traversal.append(root.value)
                inOrder(root.right)
    
        def preOrder(root):
            if root:
                traversal.append(root.value)
                preOrder(root.left)
                preOrder(root.right)
